name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'Karla-ExtraLight', Everything looks good.

name

MS NID 16/17

MS NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'Karla' + 'Space' + NID 17 'ExtraLight' = NID 1 'Karla ExtraLight'.

Karla Regular (Karla-Regular.ttf)

name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'Karla-Regular', Everything looks good.

Karla Medium Regular (Karla-Medium.ttf)

name

MS NID 16/17

MS NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'Karla' + 'Space' + NID 17 'Medium' = NID 1 'Karla Medium'.

Pass

NID 6 is 'Karla-Bold', Everything looks good.

Karla ExtraBold Regular (Karla-ExtraBold.ttf)

name

MS NID 16/17

MS NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'Karla' + 'Space' + NID 17 'ExtraBold' = NID 1 'Karla ExtraBold'.

Pass

sinf

OK: There is a subs and sinf feature in the font.
